#Russian Invites [From.ThisGetName] to Faction
country_event = {
	id = russia.0
	title = russia.0.t
	desc = russia.0.d
	picture = GFX_political_deal

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Accept
		name = russia.0.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.0.o1 executed"
		if = { limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		SOV = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		SOV = { country_event = diplomatic_response.1 }
		add_ideas = S0V_russian_sphere_idea
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = SOV value > 20 }
				add = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Never
		name = russia.0.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.0.o2 executed"
		SOV = { country_event = diplomatic_response.2 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -10
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -15
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -20
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = SOV value < 0 }
				add = -5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 50
			}
		}
	}
}
#Kursk Submarine Disaster
country_event = {
	id = russia.1
	title = russia.1.t
	desc = russia.1.d
	picture = GFX_submarine
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Horrible!
		name = russia.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.1.o1 executed"
		navy_experience = 2
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -10
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		news_event = {
			hours = 6
			id = russia_news.50
		}
	}
}

#Faction members (not Belarus): Russian imperialism
country_event = {
	id = russia.5
	title = russia.5.t
	desc = russia.5.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#We will turn our back on Russia
		name = russia.5.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.5.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -10
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -15
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes }
				add = -20
			}
		}
		SOV = { remove_from_faction = ROOT }
		set_country_flag = left_CSTO
	}

	option = {	#Loyalty must stay in place
		name = russia.5.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.5.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes
				add = 30
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}
}

		name = russia.6.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.6.o1 executed"
		army_experience = 25
		navy_experience = 10
		air_experience = 10
		SOV = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		SOV = { country_event = { id = diplomatic_response.1 days = 1 } }

			base = 50
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes
				add = 15
			}
		}

#Ukraine: Russia invades Crimea!
country_event = {
	id = russia.7
	title = russia.7.t
	desc = russia.7.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	#We shall stand down.
		name = russia.7.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.7.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia.8 days = 1 }
			transfer_state = 669
			669 = { add_core_of = SOV }
			set_country_flag = UKR_returned_crimea_to_ukraine
		}
	}

	option = { #We will stand and fight!
		name = russia.7.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.7.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 10
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia.9 days = 1 }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = UKR
					type = take_state_focus
					generator = { 669 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Russia: Ukraine folds Crimea.
country_event = {
	id = russia.8
	title = russia.8.t
	desc = russia.8.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	#Excellent
		name = russia.8.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.8.o1 executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = {
				transfer_state = 669
				add_state_core = 669
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 6
			name = threat_SOV_annexiation_of_crimea
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = annexed_ukraine
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = annexed_ukraine_trade
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = UKR
				modifier = annexed_ukraine_trade
			}
		}
	}
}

#Demand Belarus' Annexation/Puppeting
country_event = {
	id = russia.10
	title = {
		trigger = { BLR = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
		text = russia.10.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { BLR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
		text = russia.10.t2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { BLR = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
		text = russia.10.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { BLR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
		text = russia.10.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = russia.10.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.10.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { BLR = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				BLR = {
					every_owned_state = {
						add_core_of = SOV
					}
				}
				annex_country = { target = BLR transfer_troops = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BLR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				BLR = {
					every_owned_state = {
						add_core_of = SOV
					}
				}
				SOV = { puppet = BLR }
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia.3 days = 1 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
	}

	#Belarus Refuses!
	option = {
		name = russia.10.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.10.o3 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { BLR = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
			SOV = { release_puppet = BLR }
			BLR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = BLR
					type = take_state_focus
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BLR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			BLR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = BLR
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = BLR modifier = betrayed_our_cause } }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.4 days = 1 } }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

##Annex Abkhazia and South Ossetia!
country_event = {
	id = russia.11
	title = russia.11.t
	desc = russia.11.d
	picture = GFX_southern_options
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#fire_only_once = yes

	##Accept the Integration
	option = {
		name = russia.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.11.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ABK }
			SOV = { set_country_flag = ABK_accepts_annexation }
			effect_tooltip = {
				ABK = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = SOV
					}
				}
				SOV = { annex_country = { target = ABK transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SOO }
			SOV = { set_country_flag = SOO_accepts_annexation }
			effect_tooltip = {
				SOO = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = SOV
					}
				}
				SOV = { annex_country = { target = SOO transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.12 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes
				add = 30
			}
		}
	}
	#Refuse the Annexation
	option = {
		name = russia.11.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.11.o2 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ABK }
			SOV = {
				set_country_flag = ABK_refused_russias_annexation
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ABK
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.13 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SOO }
			SOV = {
				set_country_flag = SOO_refused_russias_annexation
				create_wargoal = {
					target = SOO
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.13 days = 1 } }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

##Abkhazia/South Ossetia Accepts
country_event = {
	id = russia.12
	title = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = { has_country_flag = ABK_accepts_annexation }
		}
		text = russia.12.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = { has_country_flag = SOO_accepts_annexation }
		}
		text = russia.12.t2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = { has_country_flag = ABK_accepts_annexation }
		}
		text = russia.12.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = { has_country_flag = SOO_accepts_annexation }
		}
		text = russia.12.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_southern_options
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia.12.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.12.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { has_country_flag = ABK_accepts_annexation } }
			ABK = {
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_state = { NOT = { is_core_of = SOV } } }
					every_owned_state = {
						add_core_of = SOV
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = { annex_country = { target = ABK transfer_troops = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { has_country_flag = SOO_accepts_annexation } }
			SOO = {
				if = {
					limit = { any_owned_state = { NOT = { is_core_of = SOV } } }
					every_owned_state = {
						add_core_of = SOV
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = { annex_country = { target = SOO transfer_troops = yes } }
			clr_country_flag = SOO_accepts_annexation
		}
	}
}

###Russian Investments
country_event = {
	id = russia.14
	title = russia.14.t
	desc = russia.14.d
	picture = GFX_kiev_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	#Accepts
	option = {
		name = russia.14.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.14.o1 executed"
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 10 }
			modify_international_investment_effect = yes
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			country_event = { id = diplomatic_response.1 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes
				add = 15
			}
		}
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = russia.14.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.14.o2 executed"

		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = diplomatic_distance }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = diplomatic_distance }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = diplomatic_response.2 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_10_percent_influence = yes
				add = -5
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_20_percent_influence = yes
				add = -10
			}
			modifier = {
				SOV_targeted_country_has_more_than_30_percent_influence = yes
				add = -15
			}
		}
	}
}

##Play DPR,LPR or HPR
country_event = {
	id = russia.16
	title = russia.16.t
	desc = russia.16.d
	picture = GFX_sov_russianspring
	is_triggered_only = yes
	##Play DPR
	option = {
		name = russia.16.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.16.o1 executed"
		DPR = {
			change_tag_from = SOV
		}
		trigger = { country_exists = DPR }
	}
	##Play LPR
	option = {
		name = russia.16.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.16.o2 executed"
		LPR = {
			change_tag_from = SOV
		}
		trigger = { country_exists = LPR }
	}
	##Play OPR
	option = {
		name = russia.16.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.16.o3 executed"
		OPR = {
			change_tag_from = SOV
		}
		trigger = { country_exists = OPR }
	}
	##Play HPR
	option = {
		name = russia.16.o4
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.16.o4 executed"

			change_tag_from = SOV
		}
		trigger = { country_exists = HPR }
	}
	##Play No
	option = {
		name = russia.16.o5
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.16.o5 executed"
	}
}

##Annex Alaska
country_event = {
	id = russia.21
	title = russia.21.t
	desc = russia.21.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic
	is_triggered_only = yes

	##Accept the Annexation
	option = {
		name = russia.21.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.21.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = USA }
			SOV = { set_country_flag = USA_accepts_annexation }
			effect_tooltip = {
				SOV = {
					transfer_state = 814
					add_state_core = 814
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.22 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	#Refuse the Annexation
	option = {
		name = russia.21.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.21.o2 executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = USA }
			SOV = { set_country_flag = USA_refused_annexation }
			SOV = {
				add_state_core = 814
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = USA
					modifier = major_breach_of_trust
				}
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = russia.23 days = 1 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = GEO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ABK }
			annex_country = { target = ABK transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = SOO }
			annex_country = { target = SOO transfer_troops = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.50.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.50.b executed"
		GEO = {
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ABK }
			annex_country = { target = ABK transfer_troops = yes }
		}

##AI change path
country_event = {
	id = russia.61
	title = russia.61.t
	desc = russia.61.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = russia.61.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia.61.a"
		fuck_ai_russia_passive = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_CONFEDERATION_RUSSIA_PATH
			}
			russia_subjects_federation = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_THE_RED_MENACE_PATH
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_RISE_OF_RUSSIA_PATH
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 20 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_NAZBOL_RUSSIA_PATH
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 20 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_PEACEFUL_REFORM_PATH
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }

		}
	}

			name = "Ural Militia"
			regiments = {
				Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				Militia_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				Militia_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			priority = 2
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = annex_everything
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } }
			prioritize = { 676 }
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Ural Militia\" division_template = \"Ural Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
				owner = URA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } }
			set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 20 }
			set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
			change_ruling_party_effect = yes
		}

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Eduard Rossel"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/SOV/sov_rossel.dds"
			expire = "2045.1.1"
			ideology = Nat_Populism
			traits = {
				nationalist_Nat_Populism
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

#Livonia Governorate
country_event = {
	id = russia_governorate.1
	title = russia_governorate.1.t
	desc = russia_governorate.1.d
	picture = GFX_sov_empire_governorates
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.1.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
				factor = 90
			}
		}
		LIT = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_subject_agree
			set_country_flag = SOV_subject_governorate

			set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_LIT
			clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = LIT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_governorate_rf
				}
			}
			every_core_state = { add_core_of = SOV }

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 23 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 1 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia_governorate.2 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.1.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				factor = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				factor = 90
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia_governorate.3 } }
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = betrayed_our_cause } }
	}
}
#Livonia Governorate Agree

	id = russia_governorate.2

country_event = {
	id = russia_governorate.3
	title = russia_governorate.3.t
	desc = russia_governorate.3.d
	picture = GFX_sov_empire_governorates
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.3.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.3.o1 executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = betrayed_our_cause }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LIT = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			LIT = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = LIT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = { MLV = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			MLV = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = MLV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Minks Governorate
country_event = {
	id = russia_governorate.16
	title = russia_governorate.16.t
	desc = russia_governorate.16.d
	picture = GFX_sov_empire_governorates
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.16.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.16.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				add = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				BLR = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
				add = 90
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia_governorate.17 }
		}
		BLR = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_subject_agree
			set_country_flag = SOV_subject_governorate

			set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_BLR
			clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = BLR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_governorate_rf
				}
			}
			every_core_state = { add_core_of = SOV }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 23 }
				set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 1 }
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Lukashenko"
				picture = "governer_lukashenko.dds"
				ideology = Monarchist
				traits = {
					nationalist_Monarchist
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.16.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.16.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				add = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				add = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 90
			}
		}
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = BLR modifier = betrayed_our_cause } }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia_governorate.18 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.16.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.16.o3 executed"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_union_state
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				add = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				emerging_reactionaries_are_in_power = yes
				add = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 90
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = russia_governorate.19 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = russia_governorate.19
	title = russia_governorate.19.t
	desc = russia_governorate.19.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.19.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.19.o1 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		SOV = {	country_event = { id = belarus_union.9 days = 1 } }
		BLR = { set_country_flag = BLR_unionstate_agree }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BLR_cheln_trade
				}
				remove_ideas = BLR_cheln_trade
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BLR_unstable_national_currency
				}
				remove_ideas = BLR_unstable_national_currency
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BLR_unstable_national_currency2
				}
				remove_ideas = BLR_unstable_national_currency2
				}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BLR_unstable_national_currency3
				}
				remove_ideas = BLR_unstable_national_currency3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BLR_unstable_national_currency4
				}
				remove_ideas = BLR_unstable_national_currency4
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = BLR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_union_state
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia_governorate.19.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_governorate.19.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { BLR = { NOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			BLR = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = BLR
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Successful recruitment
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.1
	title = russia_wagner.1.t
	desc = russia_wagner.1.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_events
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war = yes
		has_country_flag = SOV_creativity_is_funded
	}

	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.1.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_wagner_parties

#Wagner goes to our country
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.8
	title = russia_wagner.8.t
	desc = russia_wagner.8.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.8.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.8.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25

		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 8 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SUD }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_ideas = SOV_wagner_military_advisors
		set_country_flag = SOV_sudan_wagner_flag
		SOV = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_sudan_wagner_placed
			clr_country_flag = SOV_sudan_wagner_notplaced
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.9 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = support
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			SOV = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = influence
					id = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = 500
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
			}
			SOV = {
			set_temp_variable = { modify_wagner = -2000 }
			modify_wagner_support = yes
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Wagner Light Unit"
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 4 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
			spawn_light_infantry_wagner = yes
		}
	}
	#Disagree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.8.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.8.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.10 days = 1 }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
	}
}

#Wagner goes to our country
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.15
	title = russia_wagner.15.t
	desc = russia_wagner.15.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.15.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90

		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 8 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SYR }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_ideas = SOV_wagner_military_advisors
		SOV = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_syria_wagner_placed
			clr_country_flag = SOV_syria_wagner_notplaced
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.9 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = support
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			SOV = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = influence
					id = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = 500
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_temp_variable = { modify_wagner = -2000 }
				modify_wagner_support = yes
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Wagner Light Unit"
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 4 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
			spawn_light_infantry_wagner = yes
		}
	}
	#Disagree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.15.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.15.b executed"
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.10 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
	}
}
#Wagner against Lukash
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.16
	title = russia_wagner.16.t
	desc = russia_wagner.16.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event3
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.16.a executed"
		SOV = {
			annex_country = { target = BLR transfer_troops = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
			add_to_variable = { treasury = BLR.treasury }
			add_to_variable = { debt = BLR.debt }
			add_to_variable = { int_investments = BLR.int_investments }
		}
		BLR = {
			every_owned_state = {
				add_core_of = SOV
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25

		}
	}
	#Disagree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.16.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.16.b executed"
		SOV = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = BLR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BLR
			modifier = strategic_rivals
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = strategic_rivals
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			BLR = {
				set_temp_variable = { modify_union_state = -30 }
				modify_union_state_support = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
	}
}

#Wagner against Georgia
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.17
	title = russia_wagner.17.t
	desc = russia_wagner.17.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event3
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.17.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.17.a executed"
		SOV = {
			puppet = GEO
			country_event = diplomatic_response.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25

		}

	}

	#Disagree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.17.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.17.b executed"
		SOV = {
			country_event = diplomatic_response.2
			create_wargoal = {
				target = GEO
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.20 #bUND BLYAT
	title = russia_wagner.20.t
	desc = russia_wagner.20.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event3
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Shiiiiiiet
		name = russia_wagner.20.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.20.a executed"
		trigger = {
			BLR = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexander Lukashenko"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_contracts_with_minobr }
			}
			SOV_disorg_army_script = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				country_event = {
					id = russia_wagner.41
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = WAG
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = SOV_wagner_rebeliion_flag
			WAG = {
				set_country_flag = SOV_wagner_rebeliion_flag
				transfer_state = 667
				inherit_technology = SOV
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SOV
					type = annex_everything
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_wagner_march
					days = 30
				}
				add_manpower = 10000
				country_event = {
					id = russia_wagner.21
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_wagner_start_march_tt
	}
	option = { # No Shiiiiiiet
		name = russia_wagner.20.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.20.b executed"
		trigger = {
			BLR = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Alexander Lukashenko"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_contracts_with_minobr }
			}
			SOV_disorg_army_script = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_wagner_luka_tt
			add_stability = -0.05
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = BLR }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = SOV }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_country_flag = SOV_wagner_rebeliion_flag
			BLR = {
				country_event = {
					id = russia_wagner.25
				}
			}
			news_event = {
				hours = 1
				id = russia_wagner.34
			}
			WAG = {
				every_core_state = { remove_core_of = WAG }
			}
			add_to_variable = { treasury = WAG.treasury }
			add_to_variable = { debt = WAG.debt }
			add_to_variable = { int_investments = WAG.int_investments }
			SOV = {
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Wagner Light Unit"
					disband = yes
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Wagner Group PMC"
					disband = yes
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Wagner Tank Unit"
					disband = yes
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Wagner Heavy Mechanized Unit"
					disband = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	 		}

		}
	}

#Wagner goes to our country
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.24
	title = russia_wagner.24.t
	desc = russia_wagner.24.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.24.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.24.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25

		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 8 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = LBA }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_ideas = SOV_wagner_military_advisors
		SOV = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_lybia_wagner_placed
			clr_country_flag = SOV_lybia_wagner_notplaced
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.9 days = 1 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = support
				id = "SOV"
				value = 100
			}
			SOV = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = influence
					id = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = ROOT
					value = 500
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = ROOT
					value = 100
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_temp_variable = { modify_wagner = -2000 }
				modify_wagner_support = yes
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Wagner Light Unit"
				is_locked = yes
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 4 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			spawn_light_infantry_wagner = yes
		}
	}
	#Disagree
	option = {
		name = russia_wagner.24.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.24.b executed"
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia_wagner.10 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = recent_actions_negative }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.25 #Batka Army
	title = russia_wagner.25.t
	desc = russia_wagner.25.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event4
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Bulba Army
		name = russia_wagner.25.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: russia_wagner.25.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea1 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea1 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea2 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea2 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea3 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea3 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea3
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea4 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea4 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea4
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea5 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea5 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea6 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea6 }

		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea7 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea7 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea7
		}
		if = {
			limit = { WAG = { has_idea = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea8 } }
			WAG = { remove_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea8 }
			add_ideas = SOV_wagner_pmc_idea8
		}

			BLR = {

					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }

					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 0 y = 4 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 4 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
			WAG_army_forces = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }

}

country_event = {
	id = russia_wagner.27 #Africa Army
	title = russia_wagner.27.t
	desc = russia_wagner.27.d
	picture = GFX_wagner_event2

#Jirik Crusade
country_event = {
	id = sov_nationalists.19
	title = sov_nationalists.19.t
	desc = sov_nationalists.19.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_generic
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sov_nationalists.19.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_nationalists.19.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 90
				ROOT = { is_subject_of = SOV }
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 90
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
			ROOT = {
				set_country_flag = SOV_subject_agree
				set_country_flag = SOV_subject_governorate
				SOV = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT
						autonomy_state = autonomy_governorate_rf
						end_wars = no
						end_civil_wars = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = LEB } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_LEB
				clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = SYR } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_SYR
				clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ISR } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_ISR
				clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = EGY } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GOV_EGY
				clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
				set_country_flag = copts_revolted
				remove_ideas = { EGY_Copts_is_very_satisfied_idea EGY_Copts_is_satisfied_idea EGY_Copts_are_neutral_idea EGY_Copts_are_not_satisfied_idea EGY_Copts_are_enraged_idea }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } } }
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 13 }
					set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
				}

				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 13 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			SOV = {
				puppet = ROOT
				country_event = diplomatic_response.1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sov_nationalists.19.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_nationalists.19.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				factor = 90
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				factor = 90
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = betrayed_our_cause } }
	}
}

	desc = sov_nationalists.23.d
	picture = GFX_sov_empire_herb
	is_triggered_only = yes

	##Accept the Annexation
	option = {
		name = sov_nationalists.23.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_nationalists.23.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CHI }
			SOV = { set_country_flag = CHI_accepts_annexation }
			effect_tooltip = {
				SOV = { transfer_state = 1097 }
				SOV = { transfer_state = 555 }
				SOV = { transfer_state = 1096 }
				SOV = { transfer_state = 554 }
				SOV = { transfer_state = 552 }
				SOV = { transfer_state = 1095 }
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = sov_nationalists.24 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio > 1
				}
				add = 75
			}
		}
	}
	#Refuse the Annexation
	option = {
		name = sov_nationalists.23.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_nationalists.23.b executed"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CHI }
			SOV = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_refused_annexation
				create_wargoal = {
					target = CHI
					type = take_claimed_state
				}
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = sov_nationalists.25 days = 1 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 1
				}
				add = 75
			}
		}
	}
}

#Turkmen and Afgan Case
country_event = {
	id = sov_nationalists.27
	title = sov_nationalists.27.t
	desc = sov_nationalists.27.d
	picture = GFX_sov_empire_herb
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sov_nationalists.27.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_nationalists.27.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } }
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
			ROOT = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SOV } }
					add_core_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { is_subject_of = SOV } } }
			SOV = {
				puppet = ROOT
				country_event = diplomatic_response.1
			}
		}
	}

##Operation Declared
country_event = {
	id = sov_final_strike.1
	title = sov_final_strike.1.t
	desc = sov_final_strike.1.d
	picture = GFX_declare_svo
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = SOV_the_final_strike
	}
	option = {
		name = sov_final_strike.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_final_strike.1.a"
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.05 }
		recalculate_party = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NATO_member
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = major_breach_of_trust
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				hours = 6
				id = russia_news.11
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					BLR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_war = no
					}
				}
				BLR = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.6 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = negligible_corruption
							has_idea = slight_corruption
							has_idea = modest_corruption
							has_idea = medium_corruption
						}
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.2 days = 15 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.3 days = 15 }
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { NOT = { SOV = { has_country_flag = SOV_western_sanctions } } }
				set_country_flag = SOV_western_sanctions
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SOV_western_sanctions_modifier }
				country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.7 days = 15 }
				USA = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.4 days = 1 }
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.4 days = 1 }
				}
				FRA = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.4 days = 1 }
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = { id = sov_final_strike.4 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			decrease_economic_growth = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

	title = sov_student_rallies.1.t
	desc = sov_student_rallies.1.d
	picture = GFX_stock_market
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = sov_student_rallies.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_student_rallies.1.a"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
		}
		add_stability = -0.14
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.11
		}
		POL = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } } }
				set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_elections = no }
					set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { enable_elections = 0 }
				}
				change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes

			start_civil_war = {
				PREV = {
					leave_faction = yes
				}
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.3
			}
			POL = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
	}
}
	option = {
		name = sov_student_rallies.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_student_rallies.1.b"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		remove_ideas = NATO_member
		leave_faction = yes
		add_stability = -0.06
		increase_social_spending = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } }
			set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
			change_ruling_party_effect = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.45 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.45 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
	}
}

				has_government = communism

				factor = 20
				is_guaranteed_by = SOV
			}

				factor = 20

			}
		}

				factor = 20

		}

country_event = {
	id = sov_economic.16
	title = sov_economic.16.t
	desc = sov_economic.16.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sov_economic.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_economic.16.a executed"
		add_ideas = SOV_azot_fertilizers_idea
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = trade_mission
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = trade_mission
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = sov_economic.17 days = 1 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1

			modifier = {
				THIS = { has_opinion = { target = SOV value > -20 } }
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_top5_influencer = yes
				add = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sov_economic.16.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: sov_economic.16.b executed"
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = sov_economic.18 days = 1 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}
